 First Savarna reservation and now 200 point roster system for SC / ST / OBC

 jaane kya he roster system13 point roster system kaa sidhaa sambandh college or uniwarsity main faikalti members (professor) kii bahaali or usamen aarakshan se he
 This is a roster system in which every fourth teacher of college or university is appointed in OBC, seventh teacher SC and every fourteenth teacher in ST category
 iske tahat college yaa uniwarsity ke prayek department ko ek unit mana jaataa he
 Considering the department as a unit, there is a facility to give reservation in teacher recruitment
 isamen ab tak yahi hota tha ki puri uniwarsity ko ek akeli unit maanate hue aarakshan diya jaataa tha
 In 2017, the Allahabad High Court ordered that each department be treated as a unit, not a university or college as a single unit for reservation in the job of faculty members of SC / ST or OBC
 aage maamla supreme court main gaya jahaan sheersh adaalat ne elahabaad hoicourt ke faisle ko yathaavat rakhaa
 Students and teachers took to the streets against this decision and said that this would cause a huge loss to the SC / ST and OBC sections and reduce their quota
 roster system or raajnneetilogon ke virodh or faisle kii aalochana ko dekhte hue vipakshi dalon ko bhi nayaa hathiyaar mila or unhone sarkaar ko kathghare main khadaa kar diya
 The allegation of these parties was that the government was not concerned about such a class, only then the review petition was not put in the Supreme Court

 desh kii badi aabaadi aaj bhi gaanvon main rahati he or gramin ilaakon main 'mahatma gandhi rashtriya gramin rojgaar yojana' (manaregaa) yuvaaon ko rojgaar muhaiyaa karaane kii ahm yojana he
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi's initial statement about MNREGA was in the news
 piem modi ne farvari 2015 main sansad main manaregaa par congress ko aadhe haathon liya tha
 He had said, 'my political acumen says don't stop MNREGA
 main aisi galati nahin kar saktaa hum, kyonki manaregaa aapaki (congress kii) vifaltaaon kaa jeeta-jaagta smarak he
 i will continue to beat the drum of this memorial with instruments
 'haalanki, vitt mantri arun jetali ne aam bajet pesh karne ke turant baad march 2015 main kaha tha, 'sarkaar manaregaa ke jariye rojgaar uplabdh karaane ko lekar patibaddh he
 In such a situation, there was a mixed relationship between the Modi government and the MNREGA
 aaie jaanate hai ki upie-1 ke shasankaal main shuru kii gai is yojana ko lekar modi sarkaar kitni patibaddh rahi
 What is MNREGA? MNREGA is a program to provide employment guarantee for at least 100 days in a year in rural areas
 yah 2006 main desh ke 200 jilon main amal main aayaa, jabaki 2008 se ise desh bhar main lagu kiya gaya
 In 2014, the World Bank in its report called it a unique example of rural development
 is saal sabase bada bajatvitt varsh 2018-19 main manaregaa ke liye 55 hajaar karod rupee aavantit kiye gaye
 This is the highest budget of the scheme till date
 haalanki, takneekee rup se aisa nahin he, kyonki pichley saal yani- 2017-18 main is yojana ke liye 48 hajaar karod rupee aavantit hue the or janvari 2018 main atirikt 7 hajaar karod jari kiye
 In this way also this year, MNREGA has got the same grant as the budget of the last time
 in donon saalon main manaregaa kaa bajet sabase zyada rahaa
 What was the situation in the last 3 years? After two supplementary allocations in 2016-17, the MNREGA fund had increased to 47,500 crores
 2015-16 main manaregaa ke liye 34,699 karod bajet mila or atirikt 5 hajaar kaa vaada kiya tha
 However, according to Nikhil Dey of NREGA Sangharsh Morcha and social activist Aruna Roy, only 2,000 crores were released later
 vittiya varsh 2014-15 kii baat karen to manaregaa ke liye 34,000 karod rakhe gaye the, lekin baad main ise riviz karke 31,000 karod kar diya gaya
 How much budget during the UPA regime? Just before this, UPA-II allocated Rs 33-33 thousand crore for MGNREGA in 2013-14 and 2012-13
 2011-12 or 2010-11 main 40,100-40,100 karod rupee aavantit hue
 39,100 crore in 2009-10, a budget of Rs 30,000 crore in 2008-09
 isse pehle 2007-08 main desh ke 330 jilon ke liye 12,000 karod or 2006-07 main 200 jilon ke liye 11,300 karod rupee kaa praavdhaan tha
 Has the budget actually increased? The joint report of the NREGA Sangharsh Morcha and Swaraj Abhiyan prepared on the basis of the data of the Ministry of Rural Development offers a different picture
 vittiya varsh 2017-18 kii shuruyaat tak mazdooron kii 11,646 karod rupee kii dendaree pending thi
 So despite allocating Rs 55,000 crore this year, the beginning is from a deficit
 isi tarah 2016-17 main 47,500 karod rupee ke bajet ke saamne 13,220 karod rupee kii bakaayaa dendaree thi
 In 2015-16, there was a liability of Rs 12,218 crore against a budget of Rs 34,699 crore
 2014-15 main 31,000 karod rupee ke mukaable 6,102 karod rupee bakaayaa the
 In this way, thousands of crores of rupees of MNREGA budget is being spent in ending the backlog last year
 is sarkaar main kaise prabhavit hui manaregaa?manaregaa ko lekar modi sarkaar par aarope lage hai ki unhone manaregaa main gram sabhaaon ke adhikaron ko centre ke saamne simit kar diya he
 Approved workday on estimated workday
 isse bajet prabhavit hua he
 According to the Swaraj Abhiyan report, there were an estimated 288 crore workdays in 2017-18, while only 215 crore of these were approved workdays
 yani 25 fisadi kaarydiwason main kami ai
 There were 315 estimated workdays in 2016-17 as well, but the approved workdays were only 220
 yahaan 30 fisadi kaarydiwas kam ho gaye
 Non-payment on time is a big problem, besides non-payment on time is also a big problem
 sarkaar kii report main daawa kiya gaya ki vittiya varsh 2017-18 kii do shuruaati timahiyon main manaregaa kaa 85 fisadi bhugtan samay par kiya gaya
 However, two reports made out of the government's data showed that only 32 per cent of the payments were made on time this year
 2016-17 kii baat karen to sarkari aankade 42 fisadi bhugtan samay se hone kii baat karte hai, jabaki inhen aankadon se bani report main keval 21 fisadi bhugtan samay se hone kii baat saamne ai he
 What is the challenge before the government? In December 2017, research by Rajendra Narayanan of Azim Premji University and two independent researchers had revealed that 80% of the budget of MNREGA is spent in four months and only 20% of the budget is left for the remaining months
 suukhaagrast rajya kii haalat or bhi gambhir he
 During a hearing on a PIL in May 2016, the Supreme Court had directed the central government to immediately give MNREGA funds to 12 drought-hit states
 2015 or 2016 main sookhe ke kaaran gramin ilaakon se kai log shaharon kii ore palaayan kar gaye

 kai report main saamne aayaa he ki notebandi se gaanvon se lekar shaharon tak anskild lebar ke bich berogari badi he
